Day[1]
__________________________________________________________________________

Temp(Day[1])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.TempMean,InputClimate.TempSD,Day)=1
Precip(Day[1])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.PrecipMean,InputClimate.PrecipSD,Day)=1


PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])=Precip*(InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])/sum(InputFieldSize.FieldSize)=1/(1/1)=1

DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=(PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1]))*((WaterInField(FieldNum[1])/WaterInFieldMax(FieldNum[1]))^Beta)=(1+0)*((0/1)^1) = 0

WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1])-DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=1+0-0=1

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])+WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=0+1=1

EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(InputCropEvapTrans(CropInField(FieldNum[1],Day)*InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])),WaterInField(FieldNum[1]))=min(0,1*1,1)=min(0,1,1)=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-sum(IrrigOfField)=0-0=0

PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(PercFromFieldFrac*(WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])),(WaterInAquiferMax-WaterInAquifer))=min(1*(1-0,1),10-0)=min(0,9,10)=0,9

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=1-0,9=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer+sum(PercFromField)=0+0,9=0,9
LeakAquifer=LeakAquiferFrac*WaterInAquifer=0*0,9=0,0
WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-LeakAquifer=0,9-0,0=0,9

Precip(Day[78])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.PrecipMean,InputClimate.PrecipSD,Day)=1


PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])=Precip*(InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])/sum(InputFieldSize.FieldSize)=1/(1/1)=1

DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=(PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1]))*((WaterInField(FieldNum[1])/WaterInFieldMax(FieldNum[1]))^Beta)=(1+0)*((1,0/1)^1) = 1

WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1])-DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=1+0-1=0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])+WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=1,0+0=1,0

EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(InputCropEvapTrans(CropInField(FieldNum[1],Day)*InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])),WaterInField(FieldNum[1]))=min(0,1*1,1,0)=min(0,1,1,0)=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-sum(IrrigOfField)=10,0-0=10,0

PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(PercFromFieldFrac*(WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])),(WaterInAquiferMax-WaterInAquifer))=min(1*(1,0-0,1),10-10,0)=min(0,9,0,0)=0,0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=1,0-0,0=1,0

LeakAquifer=LeakAquiferFrac*WaterInAquifer=0*10,0=0,0
WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-LeakAquifer=10,0-0,0=10,0

Temp(Day[91])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.TempMean,InputClimate.TempSD,Day)=1
Precip(Day[91])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.PrecipMean,InputClimate.PrecipSD,Day)=1


PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])=Precip*(InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])/sum(InputFieldSize.FieldSize)=1/(1/1)=1

DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=(PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1]))*((WaterInField(FieldNum[1])/WaterInFieldMax(FieldNum[1]))^Beta)=(1+0)*((1,0/1)^1) = 1

WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1])-DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=1+0-1=0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])+WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=1,0+0=1,0

EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(InputCropEvapTrans(CropInField(FieldNum[1],Day)*InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])),WaterInField(FieldNum[1]))=min(0,1*1,1,0)=min(0,1,1,0)=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-sum(IrrigOfField)=10,0-0=10,0

PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(PercFromFieldFrac*(WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])),(WaterInAquiferMax-WaterInAquifer))=min(1*(1,0-0,1),10-10,0)=min(0,9,0,0)=0,0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=1,0-0,0=1,0

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer+sum(PercFromField)=10,0+0,0=10,0
LeakAquifer=LeakAquiferFrac*WaterInAquifer=0*10,0=0,0
WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-LeakAquifer=10,0-0,0=10,0

Temp(Day[104])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.TempMean,InputClimate.TempSD,Day)=1
Precip(Day[104])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.PrecipMean,InputClimate.PrecipSD,Day)=1


PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])=Precip*(InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])/sum(InputFieldSize.FieldSize)=1/(1/1)=1

DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=(PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1]))*((WaterInField(FieldNum[1])/WaterInFieldMax(FieldNum[1]))^Beta)=(1+0)*((1,0/1)^1) = 1

WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1])-DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=1+0-1=0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])+WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=1,0+0=1,0

EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(InputCropEvapTrans(CropInField(FieldNum[1],Day)*InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])),WaterInField(FieldNum[1]))=min(0,1*1,1,0)=min(0,1,1,0)=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-sum(IrrigOfField)=10,0-0=10,0

PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(PercFromFieldFrac*(WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])),(WaterInAquiferMax-WaterInAquifer))=min(1*(1,0-0,1),10-10,0)=min(0,9,0,0)=0,0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=1,0-0,0=1,0

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer+sum(PercFromField)=10,0+0,0=10,0
LeakAquifer=LeakAquiferFrac*WaterInAquifer=0*10,0=0,0
WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-LeakAquifer=10,0-0,0=10,0

Temp(Day[117])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.TempMean,InputClimate.TempSD,Day)=1
Precip(Day[117])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.PrecipMean,InputClimate.PrecipSD,Day)=1


PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])=Precip*(InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])/sum(InputFieldSize.FieldSize)=1/(1/1)=1

DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=(PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1]))*((WaterInField(FieldNum[1])/WaterInFieldMax(FieldNum[1]))^Beta)=(1+0)*((1,0/1)^1) = 1

WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1])-DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=1+0-1=0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])+WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=1,0+0=1,0

EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(InputCropEvapTrans(CropInField(FieldNum[1],Day)*InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])),WaterInField(FieldNum[1]))=min(0,1*1,1,0)=min(0,1,1,0)=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-sum(IrrigOfField)=10,0-0=10,0

PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(PercFromFieldFrac*(WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])),(WaterInAquiferMax-WaterInAquifer))=min(1*(1,0-0,1),10-10,0)=min(0,9,0,0)=0,0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=1,0-0,0=1,0

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer+sum(PercFromField)=10,0+0,0=10,0
LeakAquifer=LeakAquiferFrac*WaterInAquifer=0*10,0=0,0
WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-LeakAquifer=10,0-0,0=10,0

Day[130]

Temp(Day[130])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.TempMean,InputClimate.TempSD,Day)=1
Precip(Day[130])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.PrecipMean,InputClimate.PrecipSD,Day)=1


PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])=Precip*(InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])/sum(InputFieldSize.FieldSize)=1/(1/1)=1

DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=(PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1]))*((WaterInField(FieldNum[1])/WaterInFieldMax(FieldNum[1]))^Beta)=(1+0)*((1,0/1)^1) = 1

WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1])-DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=1+0-1=0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])+WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=1,0+0=1,0

EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(InputCropEvapTrans(CropInField(FieldNum[1],Day)*InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])),WaterInField(FieldNum[1]))=min(0,1*1,1,0)=min(0,1,1,0)=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-sum(IrrigOfField)=10,0-0=10,0

PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(PercFromFieldFrac*(WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])),(WaterInAquiferMax-WaterInAquifer))=min(1*(1,0-0,1),10-10,0)=min(0,9,0,0)=0,0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=1,0-0,0=1,0

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer+sum(PercFromField)=10,0+0,0=10,0
LeakAquifer=LeakAquiferFrac*WaterInAquifer=0*10,0=0,0
WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-LeakAquifer=10,0-0,0=10,0

Day[143]
__________________________________________________________________________

Temp(Day[143])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.TempMean,InputClimate.TempSD,Day)=1
Precip(Day[143])=Random.Normal(InputClimate.PrecipMean,InputClimate.PrecipSD,Day)=1


PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])=Precip*(InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])/sum(InputFieldSize.FieldSize)=1/(1/1)=1

DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=(PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1]))*((WaterInField(FieldNum[1])/WaterInFieldMax(FieldNum[1]))^Beta)=(1+0)*((1,0/1)^1) = 1

WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=PrecipOnField(FieldNum[1])+IrrigOfField(FieldNum[1])-DirectRunoff(FieldNum[1])=1+0-1=0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])+WaterInput(FieldNum[1])=1,0+0=1,0

EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(InputCropEvapTrans(CropInField(FieldNum[1],Day)*InputFieldSize.FieldSize(FieldNum[1])),WaterInField(FieldNum[1]))=min(0,1*1,1,0)=min(0,1,1,0)=0,1

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-sum(IrrigOfField)=10,0-0=10,0

PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=min(PercFromFieldFrac*(WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-EvapTransFromField(FieldNum[1])),(WaterInAquiferMax-WaterInAquifer))=min(1*(1,0-0,1),10-10,0)=min(0,9,0,0)=0,0

WaterInField(FieldNum[1])=WaterInField(FieldNum[1])-PercFromField(FieldNum[1])=1,0-0,0=1,0

WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer+sum(PercFromField)=10,0+0,0=10,0
LeakAquifer=LeakAquiferFrac*WaterInAquifer=0*10,0=0,0
WaterInAquifer=WaterInAquifer-LeakAquifer=10,0-0,0=10,0
